## Umbrella goal

**Apply to jobs.** Track A (Pipeline UX), Track B (Discovery + notifications), Track C (Profile + resume + GitHub) are all in production. Forward motion runs through real-world use AND a fresh wave of bullet/scratchpad UX work designed 2026-05-25 (S7.10–S7.13 → M7.7/M7.8/M8.6) to make the bullet-edit experience cleaner and let the resume-gen step synthesize bullets from user-voice scratchpad text when the structured profile under-covers a posting.

1. Build M7.7 → M7.8 → M8.6 in order (see "Immediate next actions").
2. Send applications.
3. When the LLM rewrites are off, capture the failure mode as a Promptfoo fixture under `eval/suites/<callsite>.yaml` and tighten the prompt.
4. When something in the pipeline misfires (wrong status classification, missed posting, calendar sync glitch), file it as a follow-up and patch.

Backups encrypted (RAH-13). Rate limits in place (RAH-12). Older MA/MB/M7/M8/M9 milestone scaffolding is shipped; consult `docs/implementation.md` for per-milestone detail.

## Critical path — current

**Apply, observe, iterate — now backed by structured LLM tracing.** The "apply ASAP" loop is fully closed (capture, kanban + side-track kanban, drill-in, contacts, watchlists, notifications with negative-filter + quiet hours, profile + multi-resume import + snapshots, tailored PDF + DOCX + skills-gap + resume-diff). 2026-05-24 added the LLM observability rail on top: every Gemini call lands in Lunary with `name` + tokens + latency when `LUNARY_PUBLIC_KEY` is set; prompt regressions catch in `npm run test:prompts` via Promptfoo. §Prompt tuning's free-text observations fold into Promptfoo fixtures going forward — see `eval/suites/<callsite>.yaml` and `docs/llm-prompts/<slug>.md`.

Disable after harvest with a vanilla `pm2 restart` (no `--update-env`).

Build a destructive-overwrite confirm + transactional bulk-replace of `WorkRole` / `Project` / `Education` from the stored payload. Pick up when you've actually made an edit you want to undo.
6. **Close-detection probe gate — ✅ SHIPPED + ARCHIVED (2026-05-30).** Live + regression-free on both tiers (5 days of clean `[job-watcher] probe-gate` logs; LinkedIn-24h / Workday-page-cap candidates confirmed *preserved*, never false-closed). ## Audit-found soft bugs (deferred — pick next)

From the 2026-05-24 system audit (commits `4a609df`, `4f1854d`, `dde9151`, `86f5aec`). Each was caught + flagged but not fixed in-session because impact was bounded or the fix required a product call. **Regression tests for the 7 fixed bugs are now in pre-push** (`job-watcher-classifier-regression-smoke`, `job-watcher-scale-regression-smoke`, `fetcher-partial-regression-smoke`, `events-broadcast-regression-smoke` — covers A/B/C/D/E/G; F is wrap-and-test-resistant). The list below is what to fix next.

| # | Issue | Where | Impact | Fix shape |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| 1 | **`nextSteps` wipe on email update.** `lib/applications/ingest.ts:208` does `nextSteps: parsed.nextSteps ?? null` — a newer email that omits nextSteps wipes the prior value (e.g. "Reply by Friday" hint disappears when the followup "we received it" email lands). | `lib/applications/ingest.ts:208` + similar in race-loser branch ~264. | Soft UX. User may lose actionable hints. | Either `nextSteps: parsed.nextSteps ?? existingApp.nextSteps` (preserve), or product call: "latest email is source of truth even when blank?" |
| 2 | **No Notification retention.** WebhookDelivery has 30d retention; Notification has none. 784 rows in 4 days currently; grows unbounded. | `prisma/schema.prisma:Notification` + `scheduler/jobs/`. | Cosmetic table bloat. Bell stays usable but DB grows. | New `scheduler/jobs/notification-prune.ts` mirroring `webhook-delivery-prune.ts`, 90-day default; wire into `scheduler/index.ts:JOBS`. |
| 3 | **Gmail webhook doesn't paginate `gmail.users.history.list`.** For active users (sparse delta per webhook) this never matters. For backfill bursts (fresh user with many historical inbox events), page 2+ records silently drop — `lastSyncedHistoryId` advances past them. | `app/api/gmail/webhook/route.ts:95-100`. | Backfill-only. Unfair to new users on signup. | Loop on `nextPageToken` from `historyRes.data.nextPageToken`, append messages, stop when no token. |
| ~~4~~ | ~~**email-parser hardcodes `"gemini-3.1-flash-lite"` in three places.**~~ Fixed 2026-05-27 in code-health sweep. Single `MODEL_ID` constant at top of `lib/email-parser.ts`; all three usages (FIXTURE log, Lunary trace `extra.model`, SDK call) read from it. | — | — | — |
| 5 | **`bulkMoveApplicationsTrack` `NOT: { id: { in: ids } }` could P2029.** Same 999-param notIn limit as Bug C. Currently bounded by UI selection size (kanban). | `lib/repositories/applications.ts:192`. | Latent — only fires if a script bulk-moves >1000 apps. | Same pattern as Bug C fix: SELECT conflicting rows, diff in JS, UPDATE by id. |
| 6 | **Scheduler ↔ Next.js cross-process race.** `processOne`'s in-process Map mutex doesn't span processes. A user clicking "Run now" while the scheduler ticks the same watchlist → both processes fetch externally + write. P2002 fallback handles per-posting collisions; the external fetch is wasted. | `scheduler/jobs/job-watcher.ts:73-82` + `app/api/watchlists/[id]/run/route.ts`. | Wasteful (duplicate fetch, potential 429 on the external source) but not corrupting. | Move the mutex to DB (`Watchlist.inFlightAt` timestamp + 60s lease), or accept it. |
| 7 | **Resume gen orphan rows on crash mid-write.** `app/api/resumes/route.ts:219-282` creates a row with `status="ready"` then writes the artifact and updates `artifactPath`. Server crash between the two leaves a "ready" row with null path — `/download` 404s while the row sits in the list. | `app/api/resumes/route.ts:219-282`. | Low probability (~100ms window). User-visible: orphan row in resume history. | Either create row with `status="generating"` and only flip to `"ready"` after artifact write succeeds, or add a startup sweep that errors-out any `status="ready" + artifactPath=null` rows. |
| 8 | **4659 legacy null-`employmentType` rows in prod.** Most pre-date the classifier or were wiped by the (now-fixed) Bug A. Not recoverable without paid backfill. | `prisma/prod.db`. | UI shows "Unspecified" for these rows. Going-forward fix is in place; backfill is one-time. | Optional: `scripts/archive/migrations/backfill-employment-types.ts` that batches the 4659 nulls through `classifyEmploymentTypes`. ~$0.50–$2 in Gemini spend. |
| ~~9~~ | ~~**`cache.ts` L1 pruner setInterval startup-skip pattern.**~~ Fixed 2026-05-27 in code-health sweep. Added a `setTimeout(pruneExpiredL1, 0)` next-tick kick before the setInterval; mirrors scheduler/index.ts's pattern. | — | — | — |
| ~~10~~ | ~~**Module-init `LUNARY_ENABLED` reads in `lib/email-parser.ts` + `lib/ai/gemini.ts`.**~~ Fixed 2026-05-27 in code-health sweep. Both modules now use a `lunaryEnabled()` function (matching `lib/ai/prompts.ts:lunaryEnabled`); `gemini.ts`'s `tracedGenerate` became a function that lazily builds + memoizes the wrapped generator on first traced call, so processes that never enable Lunary never pay the wrapModel cost. | — | — | — |

Recommended fix order if working through the list:
- ~~**Quick wins (≤ 15 min each):** #4, #9, #10.~~ Shipped 2026-05-27 as a code-health sweep.
- **High-value (~30 min):** #2 (notification-prune job), #5 (bulkMoveApplicationsTrack notIn rewrite).
- **Real product calls:** #1 (nextSteps wipe semantics), #7 (orphan-row recovery strategy).
- **Bigger lifts:** #3 (Gmail pagination — needs a backfill smoke), #6 (cross-process mutex — moves state to DB), #8 (paid backfill — needs user opt-in for spend).

**Note: every other shippable 🔴/🟡/🔵 story (and both open RAH-N items) is now ✅ or ⛔.** The backlog moves to "real-world use → first applied posting → iterate on prompts." Failure modes captured via the Lunary trace and folded into Promptfoo fixtures rather than free-text in §Prompt tuning. Genuine MVP-followup TODOs from prior sessions (LLM fuzzy bullet dedup, LinkedIn export ZIP, legacy `.doc`, per-file SSE progress, ProjectCard portfolio toggle UI) are still around but none of them block applying.

It's chmod-600 locally, but losing the Mac without an offsite copy means every encrypted backup is unrecoverable. After the 2026-05-25 slug renames (`bullet-auto-tag` → `bullet-tags-from-posting`, `bullet-tag-suggest` → `bullet-tags-from-profile`), historic traces stay on the old names until manual cleanup in Lunary's UI.
- **Push renamed prompt templates to Lunary** with `LUNARY_SECRET_KEY=… npx tsx scripts/sync-lunary-templates.ts` so dashboard slugs match codebase slugs (`resume-tagline` + `posting-parse` haven't been pushed since the 2026-05-26 M8.7 prompt edits either).

## Recently completed

- **2026-06-02 (arXiv 429 recovery — cooldown circuit breaker, committed to main, UNPUSHED)** — The shipped 3-layer fix only reduced load; it never recovered once arXiv IP-throttled us (429 → 500 → uncached → reload re-pokes → block never clears). Added a cross-tier cooldown (`arxiv_cooldown` row in the shared bucket file + per-process fallback): `noteArxivRateLimited()` trips it on any 429/"Rate exceeded", `acquireArxivSlot()` fast-fails for 15 min (env `ARXIV_COOLDOWN_MS`) so BOTH tiers go quiet and the block clears. NEW `lib/arxiv/{errors,fetch}.ts` consolidate every arXiv caller through `fetchArxivXml`; `withSharedCache` gained `fallbackOnError` to serve `[]` (200, uncached) instead of 500 on cold-cache arXiv-down. Bucket smoke 12/12, shared-cache 14/14, tsc clean; live dev :4101 all research routes 200 + this-week picks persisted (Layer 2 engaged). See top of Last session.

- **2026-05-29 (LinkedIn watchlist burst-pacing — durable scheduler fix, committed this session, UNPUSHED)** — `runDueWatchlists` (`scheduler/jobs/job-watcher.ts`) now inserts a jittered 3–10s gap before each 2nd+ crawl to a fragile scraped source (LinkedIn/Indeed; ATS APIs unaffected) so a synced batch — esp. every overdue watchlist firing on the first tick after a >cadence scheduler downtime — can't burst. Injectable (`RunDueDeps`) for hermetic testing; new `job-watcher-crawl-pacing-smoke.ts` (19 assertions) in pre-push; full gate 85/85. Paired with 4 new no-degree "side" watchlists (AI coding evaluator / math tutor / bilingual CS / junior dev) in dev.db + prod.db, desync'd via distinct prime cadences (233/239/241/251) + next-due phase stagger. Deployed live to both scheduler tiers (tsx-on-source restart). Left the parallel "hide watchlists" tree changes untouched.
- **2026-05-29 (SPA / embedded-JSON posting-text fallback, commit `815da88` — UNPUSHED)** — Client-rendered ATS pages (Dayforce et al.) returned 0 visible chars to `fetchVisibleText`, so resume-from-URL failed the `MIN_POSTING_TEXT_CHARS` guard. New `extractPostingTextFromHtml(html)` in `lib/resumes/posting.ts` falls back to embedded posting JSON (`<script type="application/ld+json">` JobPosting + Next.js `__NEXT_DATA__`) when the DOM is empty, anchoring on the `jobTitle`+`jobPostingContent` pair so it won't grab the i18n string dictionary. New `posting-spa-extract-smoke.ts` (7/7). Live Dayforce recovery 0→5507 chars. **Prod needs `npm run build` + `pm2 restart mission-control`.**
- **2026-05-28 (LLM cost optimization — Tier 1 + Tier 2, commits `d61c249` + `3b491ac`)** — Tier 1: content-keyed cache on `parsePosting` + skip-synthesis guard on solo import (eliminates the single most expensive call on the common first-import path); merged `llm-calls` docs to HTML. Tier 2: parallelized `resume-rewrite` ∥ `resume-tagline` (no data dependency), batched `scratchpad-synth` N→1 via positional output. Hermetic 79/79; Promptfoo `scratchpad-synth` 4/4 vs real Gemini; Lunary template synced + prod redeployed.
- **2026-05-27 (code-health sweep — audit bugs #4 + #9 + #10)** — Three latent maintenance hazards from the 2026-05-24 audit, fixed as one bundled commit. #4: `lib/email-parser.ts` model string `"gemini-3.1-flash-lite"` was hardcoded in three sites (FIXTURE log, Lunary `extra.model`, SDK call); pulled to a single `MODEL_ID` constant so future model bumps can't make the trace lie. #9: `lib/cache.ts` L1 pruner gained a `setTimeout(pruneExpiredL1, 0)` next-tick kick before the 5min setInterval — mirrors scheduler/index.ts's pattern; early-expiring entries no longer survive a full interval beyond their TTL. #10: both `lib/email-parser.ts` and `lib/ai/gemini.ts` had module-init `LUNARY_ENABLED` reads; converted to call-time `lunaryEnabled()` functions matching `lib/ai/prompts.ts:lunaryEnabled`. `gemini.ts`'s `tracedGenerate` became a function that lazily builds + memoizes the wrapModel-wrapped generator on first traced call, so processes that never enable Lunary never pay the wrap cost. 74/74 green; no new smokes needed (covered by existing prompt-render + tagline-draft suites which exercise both code paths).
- **2026-05-27 (Languages + Hobbies always-show + extras side-by-side render)** — User noticed generated resumes never showed their Spanish/French/German fluency or Creative Film Writing hobby. Root cause: `selectProfileExtras` was posting-keyword-filtering ALL three extras sections (skills / languages / hobbies), so for an off-domain posting (security-guard role × tech profile) every section dropped to empty. M8.7's design intent was to tailor Skills to the posting (defensible for long lists) but the same filter on Languages/Hobbies was overreach — those are credential/personality signals that should always render. Fix: filter dropped for Languages and Hobbies (always shown); Skills filter unchanged. Companion template change: the three extras sections now render as a single `extras-row` flex block so a 3-skill list + 4-language list + 1-hobby line sit side-by-side instead of eating 3 × (heading + content) vertical lines. `flex-wrap` lets any oversized section overflow to a new row. New `profile-extras-filter-smoke.ts` (9 assertions) wired into pre-push. 74/74 green.

- **Legacy `.doc`** — mammoth handles `.docx` only. Either skip or wire a converter.
- **`viewHue: 280`** for Profile dash is a placeholder — easy one-liner change in `components/providers/state/index.ts`.
- **Profile UI: per-entity `pinKeywords` chip-list editor.** 2026-05-26 backend shipped (schema migration `20260526220116_add_pin_keywords_to_entities`, Zod schemas, repository read/write, API routes, scorer keep-always + position-0 reorder, one-page pruner unremovable extension, hermetic select-smoke still 14/14). UX gap: no UI yet — users set pins via `scripts/set-entity-pin-keywords.ts` (list / set / clear). Need a chip-list affordance on WorkRoleRow / ProjectsCard rows / EducationCard rows, parallel to the bullet-tag chip pattern in BulletRow.tsx. Lives at the entity header (alongside title/company/dates). Wires into the existing PATCH endpoints — Zod schemas already accept `pinKeywords` on the request body. **Also: apply same migration to `prisma/prod.db`** via `DATABASE_URL=file:./prod.db npx prisma migrate deploy` (with prod tier paused) before this feature reaches prod resume gens.
- **Commodity-only entity penalty (resume scoring change #3).** Planned 2026-05-26. Sibling to the just-shipped keyword-importance weighting (`posting-parse` now emits `{keyword, importance}` per keyword; `scoreBullet` multiplies its base by `importance`). The penalty addresses the residual case where an entity racks up score on commodity keywords (`JavaScript`, `Web Applications`, `Full-stack Development` — importance 1–2) while another entity has fewer matches but on differentiator keywords (`Space Systems`, `ITAR` — importance 5). Today, DomeIQ (3 commodity matches on the top bullet) can still outscore Iris (2 differentiator matches per bullet) even with weighting, because count × small-weight > count × big-weight when the count gap is wide enough. Design: per-entity, compute `differentiatorShare = sum(weight ≥ 4 matches) / sum(all matches)`. If `differentiatorShare < 0.25` AND the posting has at least one keyword with `weight ≥ 4`, apply a haircut (multiplier in [0.5, 0.85] proportional to share). Open product calls: (a) is 0.25 the right threshold, or should it be the share of TOTAL posting weight (i.e. posting has 10 importance-5 points; entity hits 0 of them → big haircut, hits 5 of them → small haircut); (b) should the haircut be linear or step (e.g. 0.7 if below threshold, else 1.0); (c) do locked bullets opt out (they're user-pinned, shouldn't be score-suppressed). Implement in `lib/resumes/select.ts:scoreBullet` or a post-scoring pass in `selectFor`. Verify by re-running Rocket Lab generate — expectation: Iris ranks at or above DomeIQ.
